*/\n@Component(\"direct\")\npublic class DirectComponent extends DefaultComponent {\n\n    // active consumers\n    private final Lock consumersLock = new ReentrantLock();\n    private final Condition consumersCondition = consumersLock.newCondition();\n    private final Map<String, DirectConsumer> consumers = new HashMap<>();\n    // counter that is used for producers to keep track if any consumer was added/removed since they last checked\n    // this is used for optimization to avoid each producer to get consumer for each message processed\n    // (locking via synchronized, and then lookup in the map as the cost)\n    // consumers and producers are only added/removed during startup/shutdown or if routes is manually controlled\n    private volatile int stateCounter;\n\n    @Metadata(label = \"producer\", defaultValue = \"true\")\n    private boolean block = true;\n    @Metadata(label = \"producer\", defaultValue = \"30000\")\n    private long timeout = 30000L;\n\n    public DirectComponent() {\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected Endpoint createEndpoint(String uri, String remaining, Map<String, Object> parameters) throws Exception {\n        DirectEndpoint endpoint = new DirectEndpoint(uri, this);\n        endpoint.setBlock(block);\n        endpoint.setTimeout(timeout);\n        setProperties(endpoint, parameters);\n        return endpoint;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doShutdown() throws Exception {\n        ServiceHelper.stopAndShutdownService(consumers);\n        consumers.clear();\n        super.doShutdown();\n    }\n\n    public boolean isBlock() {\n        return block;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * If sending a message to a direct endpoint which has no active consumer, then we can tell the producer to block\n     * and wait for the consumer to become active.\n     */\n    public void setBlock(boolean block) {\n        this.block = block;\n    }\n\n    public long getTimeout() {\n        return timeout;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * The timeout value to use if block is enabled.\n     */\n    public void setTimeout(long timeout) {\n        this.timeout = timeout;\n    }\n\n    int getStateCounter() {\n        return stateCounter;\n    }\n\n    public void addConsumer(String key, DirectConsumer consumer) {\n        consumersLock.lock();\n        try {\n            if (consumers.putIfAbsent(key, consumer) != null) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n                        \"Cannot add a 2nd consumer to the same endpoint: \" + key\n                                                   + \". DirectEndpoint only allows one consumer.\");\n            }\n            // state changed so inc counter\n            stateCounter++;\n            consumersCondition.signalAll();\n        } finally {\n            consumersLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void removeConsumer(String key, DirectConsumer consumer) {\n        consumersLock.lock();\n        try {\n            consumers.remove(key, consumer);\n            // state changed so inc counter\n            stateCounter++;\n            consumersCondition.signalAll();\n        } finally {\n            consumersLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    protected DirectConsumer getConsumer(String key, boolean block, long timeout) throws InterruptedException {\n        consumersLock.lock();\n        try {\n            DirectConsumer answer = consumers.get(key);\n            if (answer == null && block) {\n                StopWatch watch = new StopWatch();\n                for (;;) {\n                    answer = consumers.get(key);\n                    if (answer != null) {\n                        break;\n                    }\n                    long rem = timeout - watch.taken();\n                    if (rem <= 0) {\n                        break;\n                    }\n                    consumersCondition.await(rem, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);\n                }\n            }\n            return answer;\n        } finally {\n            consumersLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n}\n","numLines":154,"startLine":1,"totalLines":154}}}

component.getStateCounter();\n                consumer = component.getConsumer(key, block, timeout);\n            }\n            if (consumer == null) {\n                if components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixEndpoint.java\n```java\n@UriEndpoint(firstVersion = \"4.18.0\", scheme = \"fix\", title = \"FIX\", syntax = \"fix:sessionID\",\n             category = { Category.MESSAGING, Category.FINANCE }, headersClass = FixConstants.class)\npublic class FixEndpoint extends DefaultEndpoint {\n    @UriPath(description = \"Session ID\")\n    @Metadata(required = true)\n    private String sessionID;\n\n    @UriParam\n    private FixConfiguration configuration;\n\n    public FixEndpoint() {\n    }\n\n    public FixEndpoint(String uri, Component component) {\n        super(uri, component);\n    }\n\n    public FixEndpoint(String uri, FixComponent component) {\n        super(uri, component);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public FixComponent getComponent() {\n        return (FixComponent) super.getComponent();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Producer createProducer() throws Exception {\n        return new   return true;\n    }\n\n    public String getSessionID() {\n        return sessionID;\n    }\n\n    public void setSessionID(String sessionID) {\n        this.sessionID = sessionID;\n    }\n\n FixProducer extends DefaultAsyncProducer {\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixProducer.class);\n    private final FixEndpoint endpoint;\n\n    public FixProducer(FixEndpoint endpoint) {\n        super(endpoint);\n        this.endpoint = endpoint;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void process(Exchange exchange) throws Exception {\n        String messageBody = exchange.getIn().getBody(String.class);\n        FixConfiguration config = endpoint.getConfiguration();\n\n        String senderCompID = exchange.getIn().getHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, config.getSenderCompID(), String.class);\n        String targetCompID = exchange.getIn().getHeader(FixConstants.FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, config.getTargetCompID(), String.class);\n        String fixVersion = exchange.getIn().getHeader(FixConstants.FIX_VERSION, config.getFixVersion(), String.class);\n        String sessionID = endpoint.getSessionID();\n\n        if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Sending FIX message: sessionID={}, senderCompID={}, targetCompID={}, version={}, body={}\",\n                    sessionID, senderCompID, targetCompID, fixVersion, messageBody);\n        }\n\n        exchange.getOut().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SESSION_ID, sessionID);\n        exchange.getOut().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, senderCompID);\n        exchange.getOut().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, targetCompID);\n        exchange.getOut().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_VERSION, fixVersion);\n        exchange.getOut().setBody(messageBody);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback) {\n        try {\n            process(exchange);\n            callback.done(true);\n            return true;\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            exchange.setException(e);\n            callback.done(true);\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConsumer.java\n```java\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer {\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixConsumer.class);\n    private final FixEndpoint endpoint;\n\n    public FixConsumer(FixEndpoint endpoint, Processor processor) {\n        super(endpoint, processor);\n        this.endpoint = endpoint;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public FixEndpoint getEndpoint() {\n        return (FixEndpoint) super.getEndpoint();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        super.doStart();\n        FixConfiguration config = endpoint.getConfiguration();\n\n        if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Starting FIX Consumer: sessionID={}, senderCompID={}, targetCompID={}, version={}\",\n                    endpoint.getSessionID(), config.getSenderCompID(), config.getTargetCompID(), config.getFixVersion());\n        }\n        // Initialize FIX session/acceptor\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Stopping FIX Consumer: sessionID={}\", endpoint.getSessionID());\n        }\n        // Clean up FIX session/acceptor\n        super.doStop();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\nThe camel-fix component implementation follows Apache Camel's established component architecture patterns:\n\n1. **Component Registration**: The `@Component(\"fix\")` annotation and inclusion in the components parent POM enables automatic discovery and registration with Camel's component registry.\n\n2. **URI Syntax**: The URI syntax `fix:sessionID?options` follows Camel conventions where the path part (sessionID) is marked with `@UriPath` and query parameters are marked with `@UriParam`.\n\n3. **Configuration Management**:\n   - Global component-level configuration can be set on the component\n   - Each endpoint gets a clone of the configuration to ensure isolation\n   - Configuration properties are exposed through `@UriParam` annotations for dynamic URI parameter binding\n\n4. **Endpoint Categories**: The endpoint is categorized as both `MESSAGING` (protocol nature) and `FINANCE` (business domain), making it discoverable for financial trading applications.\n\n5. **Async Processing**: The producer extends `DefaultAsyncProducer` and implements both sync and async process methods, enabling Camel to route messages efficiently through the component.\n\n6. **Lifecycle Management**:\n   - Consumer implements `doStart()` for initialization and `doStop()` for cleanup\n   - Producer maintains async callback handling for non-blocking execution\n   - Endpoint properly configures consumer through `configureConsumer()` hook\n\n### Design Decisions\n\n1. **FIX Session Session timing: Optional trading hours constraints\n\n3. **Message Headers**: FIX-specific metadata is exposed through exchange headers, allowing routes to inspect and manipulate FIX properties:\n   - `CamelFixSessionId`: Current session identifier\n   - `CamelFixSenderCompId`: Message sender\n   - `CamelFixTargetCompId`: Message recipient\n   - `CamelFixVersion`: Protocol version used\n\n4. mechanisms\n   - Integration with FIX libraries (QuickFIX/J, etc.) through producer/consumer hooks\n\n### Build and Integration\n\n- **Module Registration**: Added to components/pom.xml in components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixEndpoint.java\n```java\n@UriEndpoint(firstVersion = \"4.18.0\", scheme = \"fix\", title = \"FIX\", syntax = \"fix:sessionID\",\n             category = { Category.MESSAGING, Category.FINANCE }, headersClass = FixConstants.class)\npublic class FixEndpoint extends DefaultEndpoint {\n    @UriPath(description = \"Session ID\")\n    @Metadata(required = true)\n    private String sessionID;\n\n    @UriParam\n    private FixConfiguration configuration;\n\n    public FixEndpoint() {\n    }\n\n    public FixEndpoint(String uri, Component component) {\n        super(uri, component);\n    }\n\n    public FixEndpoint(String uri, FixComponent component) {\n        super(uri, component);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public FixComponent getComponent() {\n        return (FixComponent) super.getComponent();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Producer createProducer() throws Exception {\n        return new FixProducer(this);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Consumer createConsumer(Processor processor) throws Exception {\n        FixConsumer consumer = new FixConsumer(this, processor);\n        configureConsumer(consumer);\n        return consumer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isSingleton() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isRemote() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    public String getSessionID() {\n        return sessionID;\n    }\n\n    public void setSessionID(String sessionID) {\n        this.sessionID = sessionID;\n    }\n\n    public FixConfiguration getConfiguration() {\n        if (configuration == null) {\n            try {\n                configuration = getComponent().getConfiguration().clone();\n            } catch FixProducer extends DefaultAsyncProducer {\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixProducer.class);\n    private final FixEndpoint endpoint;\n\n    public FixProducer(FixEndpoint endpoint) {\n        super(endpoint);\n        this.endpoint = endpoint;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void process(Exchange exchange) throws Exception {\n        String messageBody = exchange.getIn().getBody(String.class);\n        FixConfiguration config = endpoint.getConfiguration();\n\n        String senderCompID = exchange.getIn().getHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, config.getSenderCompID(), String.class);\n        String targetCompID = exchange.getIn().getHeader(FixConstants.FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, config.getTargetCompID(), String.class);\n        String fixVersion = exchange.getIn().getHeader(FixConstants.FIX_VERSION, config.getFixVersion(), String.class);\n        String sessionID = endpoint.getSessionID();\n\n        if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Sending FIX message: sessionID={}, senderCompID={}, targetCompID={}, version={}, body={}\",\n                    sessionID, senderCompID, targetCompID, fixVersion, messageBody);\n        }\n\n        exchange.getOut().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SESSION_ID, sessionID);\n        exchange.getOut().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, senderCompID);\n        exchange.getOut().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, targetCompID);\n        exchange.getOut().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_VERSION, fixVersion);\n        exchange.getOut().setBody(messageBody);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback) {\n        try {\n            process(exchange);\n            callback.done(true);\n            return true;\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            exchange.setException(e);\n            callback.done(true);\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConsumer.java\n```java\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer {\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixConsumer.class);\n    private final FixEndpoint endpoint;\n\n    public FixConsumer(FixEndpoint endpoint, Processor processor) {\n        super(endpoint, processor);\n        this.endpoint = endpoint;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public FixEndpoint getEndpoint() {\n        return (FixEndpoint) super.getEndpoint();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        super.doStart();\n        FixConfiguration config = endpoint.getConfiguration();\n\n        if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Starting FIX Consumer: sessionID={}, senderCompID={}, targetCompID={}, version={}\",\n                    endpoint.getSessionID(), config.getSenderCompID(), config.getTargetCompID(), config.getFixVersion());\n        }\n        // Initialize FIX session/acceptor\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Stopping FIX Consumer: sessionID={}\", endpoint.getSessionID());\n        }\n        // Clean up FIX session/acceptor\n        super.doStop();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\nThe camel-fix component implementation follows Apache Camel's established component architecture patterns:\n\n1.
